{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01B4HtZWFW6h48YrQEL1PqP9","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_011yygTBfrjigb6gGtf6X3ES","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Istio Pilot Discovery Service Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nPilot's Discovery Service is the control plane component that serves Envoy proxies with xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) configuration. It translates high-level Istio networking resources (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, Gateways) into Envoy-compatible configurations (Listeners, Routes, Clusters, Endpoints) and pushes them to connected proxies via gRPC.\n\nThe discovery service architecture comprises four tightly integrated subsystems:\n\n1. **DiscoveryServer** — The xDS gRPC server coordinating all communication\n2. **ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service)** — The stream handler managing individual proxy connections\n3. **PushContext** — An immutable configuration snapshot regenerated on each push\n4. **ServiceRegistry** — The service discovery layer feeding endpoints and services\n\n---\n\n## 1. DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**File:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` is Pilot's core gRPC implementation for Envoy's xDS APIs. It is responsible for:\n\n- **Accepting gRPC streams** from Envoy proxies via the `StreamAggregatedResources()` RPC\n- **Tracking active connections** in the `adsClients` map, keyed by connection ID\n- **Debouncing configuration changes** to avoid thundering herd pushes\n- **Limiting concurrency** of active push operations to prevent CPU/memory overload\n- **Managing push queues** that serialize updates to individual proxies\n- **Rate limiting incoming requests** to prevent resource exhaustion\n- **Caching xDS resources** to avoid re-computation for unchanged configurations\n- **Coordinating updates** between configuration watchers (Istio CRDs, K8s services) and proxy pushes\n\n### Key State\n\n```go\ntype DiscoveryServer struct {\n    Env                 *model.Environment      // Environment with config and registry\n    Generators          map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator  // Per-proxy generators\n    adsClients          map[string]*Connection  // Active proxy connections\n    adsClientsMutex     sync.RWMutex            // Protects adsClients\n    concurrentPushLimit chan struct{}           // Semaphore limiting concurrent pushes\n    RequestRateLimit    *rate.Limiter           // Throttles incoming requests\n    pushChannel         chan *model.PushRequest // Debounce buffer for updates\n    pushQueue           *PushQueue              // Queue serializing pushes per proxy\n    Cache               model.XdsCache          // Cache for generated xDS resources\n    InboundUpdates      *atomic.Int64           // Total received updates\n    CommittedUpdates    *atomic.Int64           // Updates processed and committed\n    Generators          map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator // Per-proxy config builders\n}\n```\n\n### Lifecycle and Startup\n\n**Initialization:** `NewDiscoveryServer()` creates the server with default configurations.\n\n```go\nfunc NewDiscoveryServer(env *model.Environment, clusterAliases map[string]string, debugger *krt.DebugHandler) *DiscoveryServer\n```\n\nKey initialization steps:\n1. Create buffered channels for push debouncing and queueing\n2. Initialize concurrent push limits based on `PushThrottle` feature\n3. Setup JWT key resolver for authentication\n4. Register gRPC handlers via `Register()`\n\n**Startup:** `Start()` spawns background goroutines (pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:214-220):\n\n```\nhandleUpdates()        → Debounces incoming push requests\nsendPushes()           → Processes queued pushes from pushQueue\nperiodicRefreshMetrics() → Updates push status metrics every 10s\nCache.Run()            → Runs the XDS resource cache\n```\n\n**Readiness:** `CachesSynced()` marks the server ready to accept connections after config watchers have synced.\n\n### Push Flow and Debouncing\n\nWhen configuration changes occur, the flow is:\n\n1. **ConfigUpdate()** receives a `PushRequest` and sends it to `pushChannel` with metadata about what changed\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:298-319`\n   - Tracks `InboundUpdates` counter for diagnostics\n\n2. **handleUpdates()** runs the debounce logic:\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:326-413`\n   - Waits for at least `DebounceAfter` (100ms default) of quiet time\n   - Merges multiple requests arriving during the debounce window\n   - Enforces maximum wait time of `debounceMax` (10s default) to prevent starvation\n   - Calls `Push()` once debounce conditions are met\n\n3. **Push()** initiates a full or incremental push:\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:258-283`\n   - For full pushes: regenerates `PushContext` from scratch\n   - For incremental pushes: reuses existing `PushContext`\n   - Increments `CommittedUpdates` counter\n   - Calls `AdsPushAll()` to begin broadcasting to all clients\n\nThis design prevents rapid sequential updates from causing N pushes to each proxy, instead batching them into single pushes.\n\n### Push Queuing and Concurrency Control\n\nPushes are not sent immediately to all proxies. Instead:\n\n1. **StartPush()** enqueues the push request for each connected proxy in `pushQueue`:\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:582-594`\n   - Iterates over all active clients\n   - Enqueues the push event without blocking\n\n2. **sendPushes()** drains the queue, respecting concurrency limits:\n   - Acquires a token from `concurrentPushLimit` semaphore (default: 100 concurrent pushes)\n   - Calls `pushConnection()` to send updates to one proxy\n   - Releases the token when done\n   - This prevents CPU/memory spikes from sending to thousands of proxies simultaneously\n\n### Resource Generation\n\nWhen a proxy requests or receives a push, **generators** compute the appropriate Envoy resources:\n\n```go\nGenerators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator\n```\n\nGenerators are registered per resource type (e.g., `\"rds\"`, `\"cds\"`, `\"eds\"`). The `DiscoveryServer` maintains a map allowing per-generator or per-proxy customization via the proxy's `Generator` metadata field.\n\n**Default generators** implement the `ConfigGenerator` interface from `pilot/pkg/networking/core/configgen.go`:\n\n```go\ntype ConfigGenerator interface {\n    BuildListeners(node *model.Proxy, push *model.PushContext) []*listener.Listener\n    BuildClusters(node *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) ([]*discovery.Resource, model.XdsLogDetails)\n    BuildHTTPRoutes(node *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest, routeNames []string) ([]*discovery.Resource, model.XdsLogDetails)\n    // ... and EDS, SDS, etc.\n}\n```\n\nThe generator is given the proxy's metadata and the current `PushContext`, and produces xDS `DiscoveryResponse` messages.\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Files:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go`\n\n### Stream Establishment\n\nThe ADS stream entry point is `StreamAggregatedResources()`:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) StreamAggregatedResources(stream DiscoveryStream) error\n```\n\n1. **Authentication:** Calls `s.authenticate()` to verify the client's identity\n2. **Rate limiting:** Enforces per-connection request limits via `WaitForRequestLimit()`\n3. **Context initialization:** Ensures global `PushContext` is initialized via `InitContext()`\n4. **Connection creation:** Wraps the gRPC stream in a `Connection` object\n5. **Stream handling:** Delegates to `xds.Stream()` which manages request/response loops\n\n### Connection Type\n\nThe `Connection` struct wraps the gRPC stream with proxy-specific metadata:\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection                 // Base gRPC stream handling\n    node              *core.Node   // Original Envoy node metadata\n    proxy             *model.Proxy // Parsed proxy info (IP, cluster, labels, etc.)\n    deltaStream       DeltaDiscoveryStream // For Delta XDS protocol\n    s                 *DiscoveryServer // Back-reference to server\n}\n```\n\n**Key operations:**\n\n- `Initialize()` — Parses node metadata and registers the proxy\n- `Process()` — Handles incoming discovery requests\n- `Push()` — Receives pushed updates\n- `Proxy()` — Returns the associated proxy model\n- `Close()` — Cleans up when proxy disconnects\n\n### Proxy Initialization\n\n`initConnection()` runs when the first request is received:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:240-282`\n\n1. **Parse metadata** from the Envoy node ID and metadata blob\n2. **Check cluster aliases** (for multi-cluster scenarios)\n3. **Register the connection** in `adsClients` map\n4. **Initialize proxy state** — Load workload labels, service targets, locality\n5. **Mark as initialized** — Signal that the proxy is ready for pushes\n\nThis happens only once per connection.\n\n### Request Processing\n\n`processRequest()` handles incoming `DiscoveryRequest` messages:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:139-236`\n\n1. **Parse the request type** (CDS, RDS, EDS, LDS, etc.)\n2. **Check for debug requests** (e.g., `/debug/syncz`) and handle specially\n3. **Determine what resources to send:**\n   - For ACK/NACK of previous response: check if version has changed\n   - For new subscriptions: generate all requested resources\n   - For incremental updates: track which resources the proxy is watching\n4. **Call `pushXds()`** to generate and send the response\n\nThe connection maintains a `WatchedResource` map tracking what each proxy is subscribed to.\n\n### Configuration Push to Proxy\n\n`pushConnection()` sends configuration updates to a single proxy:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:472-570`\n\n1. **Check if push is needed** — Call `ProxyNeedsPush()` to short-circuit if nothing changed\n2. **Generate resources** for each watched resource type:\n   - Call the appropriate generator (via `findGenerator()`)\n   - Generator consults `PushContext` to produce Envoy resources\n   - Resources are marshaled into `DiscoveryResponse` format\n3. **Build response** with:\n   - Generated resources\n   - New version and nonce (for tracking)\n   - Control plane identifier\n4. **Send response** via the gRPC stream\n5. **Update statistics** — Record push time, size, errors\n\n**Error handling:**\n- If generating resources fails, the error is logged and a `DiscoveryResponse` with error details is sent\n- Proxy receives the error in the response but stays connected; next push will retry\n- Errors are aggregated in `PushContext` for debugging\n\n### Broadcast to All Proxies\n\n`StartPush()` and `AdsPushAll()` trigger pushes to all connected proxies:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:550-594`\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) AdsPushAll(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    s.StartPush(req)\n}\n\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) StartPush(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    for _, p := range s.AllClients() {\n        s.pushQueue.Enqueue(p, req)\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis is called from `Push()` and enqueues a single push event for every connected proxy. The `sendPushes()` background goroutine then processes these one at a time, respecting concurrency limits.\n\n### Delta XDS Support\n\nDelta XDS is an alternative protocol that sends incremental changes (`added` and `removed` resources) instead of full resource lists. It's implemented in `delta.go` with a parallel architecture:\n\n- `DeltaAggregatedResources()` — Entry point for Delta XDS streams\n- `pushConnectionDelta()` — Similar to `pushConnection()` but tracks resource state\n- Delta responses are smaller and reduce CPU when only a few resources change\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**Files:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/context.go`\n\n### Purpose and Semantics\n\n`PushContext` is an **immutable snapshot** of the current mesh configuration at a specific point in time. All proxies receiving a push with the same `PushContext` are guaranteed to compute the same Envoy configuration.\n\nKey invariant: **Once a `PushContext` is initialized, it never changes**. Configuration updates create a new `PushContext`.\n\n### Contents\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service and traffic routing indices\n    ServiceIndex            serviceIndex\n    virtualServiceIndex     virtualServiceIndex\n    destinationRuleIndex    destinationRuleIndex\n    gatewayIndex            gatewayIndex\n    sidecarIndex            sidecarIndex\n\n    // Policies and extensions\n    AuthnPolicies          *AuthenticationPolicies\n    AuthzPolicies          *AuthorizationPolicies\n    Telemetry              *Telemetries\n    ProxyConfigs           *ProxyConfigs\n    envoyFiltersByNamespace map[string][]*EnvoyFilterWrapper\n    wasmPluginsByNamespace  map[string][]*WasmPluginWrapper\n\n    // Mesh metadata\n    Mesh                   *meshconfig.MeshConfig\n    Networks               *meshconfig.MeshNetworks\n    clusterLocalHosts      ClusterLocalHosts\n\n    // Push metadata\n    PushVersion            string // Unique identifier for this snapshot\n    JwtKeyResolver         *JwksResolver\n    GatewayAPIController   GatewayController\n\n    // Tracking\n    ProxyStatus            map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n    InitDone               atomic.Bool\n}\n```\n\n### Initialization\n\n`InitContext()` is called once per `PushContext` and populates all indices:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:1345-1373`\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest)\n```\n\nTwo paths:\n\n**Full rebuild** (on first initialization or if `Forced: true`):\n- `createNewContext()` — Rebuilds all indices from scratch\n- Called when:\n  - First connection from a proxy\n  - After mesh config changes\n  - On explicit full push requests\n\nSteps in `createNewContext()`:\n1. `initServiceRegistry()` — Index all services from K8s and ServiceEntry resources\n2. `initVirtualServices()` — Index all VirtualServices, organizing by export scope\n3. `initDestinationRules()` — Index DestinationRules with load balancing, connection pooling\n4. `initAuthorizationPolicies()` — Build access control matrix\n5. `initGateways()` — Index Gateways and manage ingress/egress rules\n6. `initSidecarScopes()` — Compute sidecar traffic routing rules\n7. ... and others (AuthnPolicies, Telemetry, WasmPlugins, EnvoyFilters)\n\n**Incremental update** (when config is partially changed):\n- `updateContext()` — Rebuilds only affected indices\n- Called when:\n  - A specific config type (e.g., VirtualService) changed\n  - ServiceEntry was added/removed\n  - DestinationRule was modified\n\n`updateContext()` examines `PushRequest.ConfigsUpdated` to determine what changed:\n```go\nfor conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated {\n    switch conf.Kind {\n    case kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DNSName:\n        servicesChanged = true\n        ps.initServiceRegistry(env, pushReq.ConfigsUpdated)\n    case kind.VirtualService:\n        virtualServicesChanged = true\n        ps.initVirtualServices(env)\n    // ... etc\n    }\n}\n```\n\nIf a type didn't change, the old index is reused.\n\n### Configuration Translation\n\nWhen generators compute Envoy configuration, they consult `PushContext` to:\n\n1. **Resolve service names** to service definitions via `ServiceIndex`\n2. **Apply routing rules** — Find matching `VirtualServices` and `DestinationRules`\n3. **Compute load balancing** — Consult `destinationRuleIndex` for connection pool and outlier detection\n4. **Filter routes** — Check `sidecarIndex` to determine what traffic a proxy should see\n5. **Apply policies** — Consult `AuthzPolicies`, `AuthnPolicies`, `Telemetry`\n6. **Extend config** — Apply `EnvoyFilters` and `WasmPlugins`\n\nExample: Translating a `VirtualService` to Envoy `RouteConfiguration`:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/routes.go` (not shown here but referenced)\n- Reads route rules from the VirtualService CRD\n- Consults `ServiceIndex` to resolve destination service hosts\n- Looks up `DestinationRule` for the destination\n- Generates Envoy `Route` with backend cluster names, weights, retries, etc.\n\n### Push Metrics and Error Tracking\n\n`PushContext` also tracks push status:\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n    // Keyed by error code (e.g., \"success\", \"timeout\"), then by proxy ID\n}\n\ntype ProxyPushStatus struct {\n    ProxyID       string\n    LastUpdateTime time.Time\n    LastError     string\n}\n```\n\nAfter each push to a proxy:\n- Success → recorded in `ProxyStatus[\"success\"]`\n- Error → recorded in `ProxyStatus[errorCode]` with error message\n- Metrics → aggregated and exposed on debug endpoints\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Files:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go`, `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller.go`\n\n### Service Discovery Architecture\n\nPilot abstracts service discovery behind a **registry** interface. The system supports multiple registries simultaneously:\n\n```go\ntype ServiceDiscovery interface {\n    Services() []*Service\n    GetService(hostname host.Name) *Service\n    InstancesByPort(hostname host.Name, port int, labels labels.Instance) []*IstioEndpoint\n    // ... etc\n}\n```\n\n### Aggregate Controller Pattern\n\nThe `Controller` in `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/` implements multi-cluster and multi-provider support:\n\n```go\ntype Controller struct {\n    registries []*registryEntry  // List of service registries (K8s, ServiceEntry, etc.)\n    handlers   model.ControllerHandlers  // Callbacks for changes\n}\n```\n\nWhen querying services:\n```go\nfunc (c *Controller) Services() []*Service {\n    var services []*Service\n    for _, reg := range c.registries {\n        services = append(services, reg.Services()...)\n    }\n    return services\n}\n```\n\nThis allows seamless aggregation of:\n- **Kubernetes registries** — One per cluster connected to this Istiod\n- **ServiceEntry resources** — Custom services defined in the mesh\n- **External service discovery** — Pluggable external systems\n\n### Kubernetes Registry\n\nThe main registry implementation for Kubernetes:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller.go`\n\nWatches:\n1. **Services** — Kubernetes `Service` objects\n2. **Endpoints** — `Endpoints` or `EndpointSlices` objects (pod membership)\n3. **Pods** — Pod objects for labels and locality information\n\nWhen a service is created/updated:\n- `SvcUpdate()` is called with the change event\n- Triggers a `PushRequest` with `ConfigsUpdated` including `kind.Service`\n- Next push will regenerate service indices and push CDS/EDS to all proxies\n\nWhen endpoints change (pod scale-up, health check failure):\n- `EDSUpdate()` is called with the updated endpoint list\n- Triggers an incremental `PushRequest` with `Full: false`\n- Only EDS is regenerated; other resource types reuse cached versions\n\n### ServiceEntry Resources\n\nServiceEntry is an Istio CRD that defines custom services:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: ServiceEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: my-service\nspec:\n  hosts:\n  - my-service.example.com\n  location: MESH_EXTERNAL\n  ports:\n  - number: 443\n    name: https\n  endpoints:\n  - address: 1.2.3.4\n    ports:\n      https: 443\n```\n\nServiceEntry acts as a \"service\" in the registry, allowing Istio to mesh traffic to external systems.\n\nA config controller watches ServiceEntry resources and calls `SvcUpdate()` when they change.\n\n### Multi-Cluster Support\n\nMulti-cluster deployments have multiple Istiod instances, each connected to one or more Kubernetes clusters. The aggregate controller handles this:\n\n```go\ntype registryEntry struct {\n    Controller model.ServiceDiscovery\n    clusterID  cluster.ID\n}\n```\n\nEach registry entry has a `clusterID`. When aggregating services:\n\n1. Services are tagged with their source cluster\n2. Endpoints include cluster locality information\n3. The aggregate controller optionally filters by cluster (e.g., for sidecar scope)\n\n**Example:** A gateway in cluster A wants to load-balance across services in clusters A, B, and C:\n- The aggregate controller returns services from all three clusters\n- Each service's endpoints are tagged with their cluster ID\n- Envoy uses cluster-aware load balancing (locality-weighted) to prefer local endpoints\n\n### Push Trigger Points\n\nThe registry triggers pushes at two levels:\n\n**1. Service Changes → Full Config Push**\n```go\ns.XDSUpdater.SvcUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, event)\n// Creates PushRequest with ConfigsUpdated = {kind.Service}\n// → Triggers InitContext to rebuild service indices\n// → Pushes CDS/RDS/EDS to all proxies\n```\n\n**2. Endpoint Changes → Incremental EDS Push**\n```go\ns.XDSUpdater.EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, endpoints)\n// Creates PushRequest with Full: false (incremental)\n// → Skips InitContext; reuses existing PushContext\n// → Pushes only EDS to affected proxies\n```\n\nThis separation is crucial for performance. Endpoint churn (pods scaling, health changes) happens frequently but only affects EDS, not routing rules.\n\n### Error Handling in Registry\n\nIf a registry fails to return services:\n- The error is logged\n- The previous service list is retained (safe-by-default)\n- Subsequent queries will retry\n- Eventually a new push will regenerate the context\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow: From Config Change to Proxy\n\nTo understand how everything works together, trace a typical flow:\n\n### Scenario: VirtualService is created\n\n1. **Controller watches CRD:**\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/config/crd/crd.go` or `pilot/pkg/config/kube/` (config watchers)\n   - Detects new VirtualService in etcd\n   - Calls `ConfigUpdater.ConfigUpdate()`\n\n2. **Push request enters debouncer:**\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:299-319`\n   - `ConfigUpdate()` sends to `pushChannel`\n   - `handleUpdates()` waits for quiet time\n\n3. **Push is triggered:**\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:258-283`\n   - `Push()` calls `initPushContext()` which:\n     - Creates new `PushContext`\n     - Calls `InitContext()` to rebuild indices\n     - `initVirtualServices()` reads all VirtualServices from config store\n   - Calls `AdsPushAll()` to queue push for all proxies\n\n4. **Each proxy receives update:**\n   - `StartPush()` enqueues event for proxy in `pushQueue`\n   - `sendPushes()` calls `pushConnection()` for proxy\n   - `pushConnection()` calls generators:\n     - CDS generator reads services and produces clusters\n     - RDS generator reads VirtualServices and DestinationRules, produces routes\n   - xDS response is sent to proxy via gRPC stream\n\n5. **Proxy processes:**\n   - Envoy receives new routes\n   - Updates its routing table\n   - Traffic is now routed according to the new VirtualService\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### 1. Custom Resource Generators\n\nReplace the default xDS generators to customize Envoy configuration:\n\n```go\ndiscoveryServer.Generators[\"my-custom-generator/cds\"] = myCustomCDSGenerator\n```\n\nCustom generators implement the `XdsResourceGenerator` interface.\n\n### 2. Custom Service Registries\n\nPlug in external service discovery:\n\n```go\naggregateController.AddRegistry(myServiceRegistry, clusterID)\n```\n\nThe aggregate controller will include services from your registry in queries.\n\n### 3. Config Watchers\n\nAdd watchers for custom resources:\n\n```go\nconfigStore.RegisterEventHandler(configUpdateHandler)\n// Handler receives ConfigUpdate events\n```\n\nPush requests will include your resource in `ConfigsUpdated`, triggering regeneration.\n\n### 4. Proxy Filtering\n\nControl which proxies need a push:\n\n```go\ndiscoveryServer.ProxyNeedsPush = myProxyFilter\n```\n\nYour filter can return early if a push is unnecessary for a specific proxy.\n\n### 5. Telemetry and Monitoring\n\nHook into push status:\n\n```go\npush.AddMetric(metric, key, proxyID, message)\n```\n\nMetrics are exposed on debug endpoints and in logs.\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Configuration Validation Errors\n\nWhen a config CRD is invalid (malformed YAML, validation failure):\n- Config controller logs the error\n- The invalid config is not added to the config store\n- Existing proxies retain their previous configuration\n- No push is triggered\n\nThis prevents invalid configs from breaking the mesh.\n\n### Push Generation Errors\n\nIf a generator fails (e.g., out of memory):\n- The error is caught in `pushConnection()`\n- A `DiscoveryResponse` with error status is sent to the proxy\n- The error is recorded in `PushContext.ProxyStatus`\n- The proxy stays connected; next push will retry\n- Error metrics are incremented\n\n### Registry Errors\n\nIf a service registry becomes unavailable:\n- Queries return cached services\n- Subsequent changes trigger retries\n- Eventually the registry recovers and new changes are processed\n\n### Proxy Connection Errors\n\nIf a proxy becomes unresponsive:\n- The stream is closed\n- The connection is removed from `adsClients`\n- The `WorkloadEntryController` is notified (cleanup auto-registered proxies)\n- Other proxies continue receiving pushes unaffected\n\n---\n\n## Performance and Scalability Considerations\n\n### Debouncing\n\nPrevents sending 100 pushes when 100 configs change in rapid succession. Instead, one debounced push is sent after quiet time.\n\nTunable via:\n- `DebounceAfter` — Quiet time threshold (default: 100ms)\n- `debounceMax` — Maximum wait time (default: 10s)\n- `enableEDSDebounce` — Whether to debounce EDS separately\n\n### Concurrent Push Limiting\n\nSemaphore prevents overwhelming CPU/memory by sending to all 10,000 proxies simultaneously.\n\nTunable via:\n- `PushThrottle` — Max concurrent pushes (default: 100)\n\n### Caching\n\nGenerated Envoy configuration is cached in `PushContext.Cache`. If nothing changed, the cache hit avoids recomputation.\n\n### Incremental Updates\n\nEDS changes don't regenerate routing configuration. Endpoint churn is common; full pushes are expensive.\n\n### Resource Indexes\n\n`PushContext` builds indices (maps) of services, VirtualServices, etc. for O(1) lookup instead of O(n) scanning.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\nCore implementation:\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` — DiscoveryServer lifecycle and push coordination\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` — ADS stream handling and per-proxy pushes\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go` — Delta XDS alternative protocol\n- `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` — PushContext initialization and indices\n- `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` — Environment and global push context management\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` — Multi-registry aggregation\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller.go` — Kubernetes service discovery\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/configgen.go` — ConfigGenerator interface definition\n- `pilot/pkg/bootstrap/server.go` — Pilot server initialization and controller setup\n\nConfig and CRD handling:\n- `pilot/pkg/config/crd/crd.go` — CRD config store\n- `pilot/pkg/config/kube/` — Kubernetes resource controllers\n\nGenerators (xDS resource translation):\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/` — VirtualService, DestinationRule translation\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` — Cluster Discovery Service (CDS) generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` — Route Discovery Service (RDS) generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` — Listener Discovery Service (LDS) generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` — Endpoint Discovery Service (EDS) generator\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nPilot's discovery service is a coordinated system where:\n\n- **DiscoveryServer** manages the overall push flow, debouncing, and concurrency\n- **ADS** handles individual proxy connections and request/response streams\n- **PushContext** provides a consistent, immutable configuration snapshot\n- **ServiceRegistry** feeds real-time services and endpoints into the context\n\nConfiguration changes trigger a push that flows through debouncing, context regeneration, resource generation, and broadcasting to all proxies. The architecture supports multi-cluster deployments, incremental updates, error recovery, and extensive customization through generators and filters.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2156,"cache_read_input_tokens":75085,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2156},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"268bba35-c03c-4134-abe7-93fb5989827b","uuid":"7903abc4-b63c-4ee5-9fa5-6b42df54e4d6"}

It translates high-level Istio networking resources (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, Gateways) into Envoy-compatible configurations (Listeners, Routes, Clusters, Endpoints) and pushes them to connected proxies via gRPC.\n\nThe discovery service architecture comprises four tightly integrated subsystems:\n\n1. **DiscoveryServer** — The xDS gRPC server coordinating all communication\n2. **ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service)** — The stream handler managing individual proxy connections\n3. **PushContext** — An immutable configuration snapshot regenerated on each push\n4. **ServiceRegistry** — The service discovery layer feeding endpoints and services\n\n---\n\n## 1. DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**File:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` is Pilot's core gRPC implementation for Envoy's xDS APIs. It is responsible for:\n\n- **Accepting gRPC streams** from Envoy proxies via the `StreamAggregatedResources()` RPC\n- **Tracking active connections** in the `adsClients` map, keyed by connection ID\n- **Debouncing configuration changes** to avoid thundering herd pushes\n- **Limiting concurrency** of active push operations to prevent CPU/memory overload\n- **Managing push queues** that serialize updates to individual proxies\n- **Rate limiting incoming requests** to prevent resource exhaustion\n- **Caching xDS resources** to avoid re-computation for unchanged configurations\n- **Coordinating updates** between configuration watchers (Istio CRDs, K8s services) and proxy pushes\n\n### Key State\n\n```go\ntype DiscoveryServer struct {\n    Env                 *model.Environment      // Environment with config and registry\n    Generators          map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator  // Per-proxy generators\n    adsClients          map[string]*Connection  // Active proxy connections\n    adsClientsMutex     sync.RWMutex            // Protects adsClients\n    concurrentPushLimit chan struct{}           // Semaphore limiting concurrent pushes\n    RequestRateLimit    *rate.Limiter           // Throttles incoming requests\n    pushChannel         chan *model.PushRequest // Debounce buffer for updates\n    pushQueue           *PushQueue              // Queue serializing pushes per proxy\n    Cache               model.XdsCache          // Cache for generated xDS resources\n    InboundUpdates      *atomic.Int64           // Total received updates\n    CommittedUpdates    *atomic.Int64           // Updates processed and committed\n    Generators          map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator // Per-proxy config builders\n}\n```\n\n### Lifecycle and Startup\n\n**Initialization:** `NewDiscoveryServer()` creates the server with default configurations.\n\n```go\nfunc NewDiscoveryServer(env *model.Environment, clusterAliases map[string]string, debugger *krt.DebugHandler) *DiscoveryServer\n```\n\nKey initialization steps:\n1. Create buffered channels for push debouncing and queueing\n2. Initialize concurrent push limits based on `PushThrottle` feature\n3. Setup JWT key resolver for authentication\n4. Register gRPC handlers via `Register()`\n\n**Startup:** `Start()` spawns background goroutines (pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:214-220):\n\n```\nhandleUpdates()        → Debounces incoming push requests\nsendPushes()           → Processes queued pushes from pushQueue\nperiodicRefreshMetrics() → Updates push status metrics every 10s\nCache.Run()            → Runs the XDS resource cache\n```\n\n**Readiness:** `CachesSynced()` marks the server ready to accept connections after config watchers have synced.\n\n### Push Flow and Debouncing\n\nWhen configuration changes occur, the flow is:\n\n1. **ConfigUpdate()** receives a `PushRequest` and sends it to `pushChannel` with metadata about what changed\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:298-319`\n   - Tracks `InboundUpdates` counter for diagnostics\n\n2. **handleUpdates()** runs the debounce logic:\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:326-413`\n   - Waits for at least `DebounceAfter` (100ms default) of quiet time\n   - Merges multiple requests arriving during the debounce window\n   - Enforces maximum wait time of `debounceMax` (10s default) to prevent starvation\n   - Calls `Push()` once debounce conditions are met\n\n3. **Push()** initiates a full or incremental push:\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:258-283`\n   - For full pushes: regenerates `PushContext` from scratch\n   - For incremental pushes: reuses existing `PushContext`\n   - Increments `CommittedUpdates` counter\n   - Calls `AdsPushAll()` to begin broadcasting to all clients\n\nThis design prevents rapid sequential updates from causing N pushes to each proxy, instead batching them into single pushes.\n\n### Push Queuing and Concurrency Control\n\nPushes are not sent immediately to all proxies. Instead:\n\n1. **StartPush()** enqueues the push request for each connected proxy in `pushQueue`:\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:582-594`\n   - Iterates over all active clients\n   - Enqueues the push event without blocking\n\n2. **sendPushes()** drains the queue, respecting concurrency limits:\n   - Acquires a token from `concurrentPushLimit` semaphore (default: 100 concurrent pushes)\n   - Calls `pushConnection()` to send updates to one proxy\n   - Releases the token when done\n   - This prevents CPU/memory spikes from sending to thousands of proxies simultaneously\n\n### Resource Generation\n\nWhen a proxy requests or receives a push, **generators** compute the appropriate Envoy resources:\n\n```go\nGenerators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator\n```\n\nGenerators are registered per resource type (e.g., `\"rds\"`, `\"cds\"`, `\"eds\"`). The `DiscoveryServer` maintains a map allowing per-generator or per-proxy customization via the proxy's `Generator` metadata field.\n\n**Default generators** implement the `ConfigGenerator` interface from `pilot/pkg/networking/core/configgen.go`:\n\n```go\ntype ConfigGenerator interface {\n    BuildListeners(node *model.Proxy, push *model.PushContext) []*listener.Listener\n    BuildClusters(node *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) ([]*discovery.Resource, model.XdsLogDetails)\n    BuildHTTPRoutes(node *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest, routeNames []string) ([]*discovery.Resource, model.XdsLogDetails)\n    // ... and EDS, SDS, etc.\n}\n```\n\nThe generator is given the proxy's metadata and the current `PushContext`, and produces xDS `DiscoveryResponse` messages.\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Files:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go`\n\n### Stream Establishment\n\nThe ADS stream entry point is `StreamAggregatedResources()`:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) StreamAggregatedResources(stream DiscoveryStream) error\n```\n\n1. **Authentication:** Calls `s.authenticate()` to verify the client's identity\n2. **Rate limiting:** Enforces per-connection request limits via `WaitForRequestLimit()`\n3. **Context initialization:** Ensures global `PushContext` is initialized via `InitContext()`\n4. **Connection creation:** Wraps the gRPC stream in a `Connection` object\n5. **Stream handling:** Delegates to `xds.Stream()` which manages request/response loops\n\n### Connection Type\n\nThe `Connection` struct wraps the gRPC stream with proxy-specific metadata:\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection                 // Base gRPC stream handling\n    node              *core.Node   // Original Envoy node metadata\n    proxy             *model.Proxy // Parsed proxy info (IP, cluster, labels, etc.)\n    deltaStream       DeltaDiscoveryStream // For Delta XDS protocol\n    s                 *DiscoveryServer // Back-reference to server\n}\n```\n\n**Key operations:**\n\n- `Initialize()` — Parses node metadata and registers the proxy\n- `Process()` — Handles incoming discovery requests\n- `Push()` — Receives pushed updates\n- `Proxy()` — Returns the associated proxy model\n- `Close()` — Cleans up when proxy disconnects\n\n### Proxy Initialization\n\n`initConnection()` runs when the first request is received:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:240-282`\n\n1. **Parse metadata** from the Envoy node ID and metadata blob\n2. **Check cluster aliases** (for multi-cluster scenarios)\n3. **Register the connection** in `adsClients` map\n4. **Initialize proxy state** — Load workload labels, service targets, locality\n5. **Mark as initialized** — Signal that the proxy is ready for pushes\n\nThis happens only once per connection.\n\n### Request Processing\n\n`processRequest()` handles incoming `DiscoveryRequest` messages:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:139-236`\n\n1. **Parse the request type** (CDS, RDS, EDS, LDS, etc.)\n2. **Check for debug requests** (e.g., `/debug/syncz`) and handle specially\n3. **Determine what resources to send:**\n   - For ACK/NACK of previous response: check if version has changed\n   - For new subscriptions: generate all requested resources\n   - For incremental updates: track which resources the proxy is watching\n4. **Call `pushXds()`** to generate and send the response\n\nThe connection maintains a `WatchedResource` map tracking what each proxy is subscribed to.\n\n### Configuration Push to Proxy\n\n`pushConnection()` sends configuration updates to a single proxy:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:472-570`\n\n1. **Check if push is needed** — Call `ProxyNeedsPush()` to short-circuit if nothing changed\n2. **Generate resources** for each watched resource type:\n   - Call the appropriate generator (via `findGenerator()`)\n   - Generator consults `PushContext` to produce Envoy resources\n   - Resources are marshaled into `DiscoveryResponse` format\n3. **Build response** with:\n   - Generated resources\n   - New version and nonce (for tracking)\n   - Control plane identifier\n4. **Send response** via the gRPC stream\n5. **Update statistics** — Record push time, size, errors\n\n**Error handling:**\n- If generating resources fails, the error is logged and a `DiscoveryResponse` with error details is sent\n- Proxy receives the error in the response but stays connected; next push will retry\n- Errors are aggregated in `PushContext` for debugging\n\n### Broadcast to All Proxies\n\n`StartPush()` and `AdsPushAll()` trigger pushes to all connected proxies:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go:550-594`\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) AdsPushAll(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    s.StartPush(req)\n}\n\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) StartPush(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    for _, p := range s.AllClients() {\n        s.pushQueue.Enqueue(p, req)\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThis is called from `Push()` and enqueues a single push event for every connected proxy. The `sendPushes()` background goroutine then processes these one at a time, respecting concurrency limits.\n\n### Delta XDS Support\n\nDelta XDS is an alternative protocol that sends incremental changes (`added` and `removed` resources) instead of full resource lists. It's implemented in `delta.go` with a parallel architecture:\n\n- `DeltaAggregatedResources()` — Entry point for Delta XDS streams\n- `pushConnectionDelta()` — Similar to `pushConnection()` but tracks resource state\n- Delta responses are smaller and reduce CPU when only a few resources change\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**Files:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/context.go`\n\n### Purpose and Semantics\n\n`PushContext` is an **immutable snapshot** of the current mesh configuration at a specific point in time. All proxies receiving a push with the same `PushContext` are guaranteed to compute the same Envoy configuration.\n\nKey invariant: **Once a `PushContext` is initialized, it never changes**. Configuration updates create a new `PushContext`.\n\n### Contents\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service and traffic routing indices\n    ServiceIndex            serviceIndex\n    virtualServiceIndex     virtualServiceIndex\n    destinationRuleIndex    destinationRuleIndex\n    gatewayIndex            gatewayIndex\n    sidecarIndex            sidecarIndex\n\n    // Policies and extensions\n    AuthnPolicies          *AuthenticationPolicies\n    AuthzPolicies          *AuthorizationPolicies\n    Telemetry              *Telemetries\n    ProxyConfigs           *ProxyConfigs\n    envoyFiltersByNamespace map[string][]*EnvoyFilterWrapper\n    wasmPluginsByNamespace  map[string][]*WasmPluginWrapper\n\n    // Mesh metadata\n    Mesh                   *meshconfig.MeshConfig\n    Networks               *meshconfig.MeshNetworks\n    clusterLocalHosts      ClusterLocalHosts\n\n    // Push metadata\n    PushVersion            string // Unique identifier for this snapshot\n    JwtKeyResolver         *JwksResolver\n    GatewayAPIController   GatewayController\n\n    // Tracking\n    ProxyStatus            map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n    InitDone               atomic.Bool\n}\n```\n\n### Initialization\n\n`InitContext()` is called once per `PushContext` and populates all indices:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:1345-1373`\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env *Environment, oldPushContext *PushContext, pushReq *PushRequest)\n```\n\nTwo paths:\n\n**Full rebuild** (on first initialization or if `Forced: true`):\n- `createNewContext()` — Rebuilds all indices from scratch\n- Called when:\n  - First connection from a proxy\n  - After mesh config changes\n  - On explicit full push requests\n\nSteps in `createNewContext()`:\n1. `initServiceRegistry()` — Index all services from K8s and ServiceEntry resources\n2. `initVirtualServices()` — Index all VirtualServices, organizing by export scope\n3. `initDestinationRules()` — Index DestinationRules with load balancing, connection pooling\n4. `initAuthorizationPolicies()` — Build access control matrix\n5. `initGateways()` — Index Gateways and manage ingress/egress rules\n6. `initSidecarScopes()` — Compute sidecar traffic routing rules\n7. ... and others (AuthnPolicies, Telemetry, WasmPlugins, EnvoyFilters)\n\n**Incremental update** (when config is partially changed):\n- `updateContext()` — Rebuilds only affected indices\n- Called when:\n  - A specific config type (e.g., VirtualService) changed\n  - ServiceEntry was added/removed\n  - DestinationRule was modified\n\n`updateContext()` examines `PushRequest.ConfigsUpdated` to determine what changed:\n```go\nfor conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated {\n    switch conf.Kind {\n    case kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DNSName:\n        servicesChanged = true\n        ps.initServiceRegistry(env, pushReq.ConfigsUpdated)\n    case kind.VirtualService:\n        virtualServicesChanged = true\n        ps.initVirtualServices(env)\n    // ... etc\n    }\n}\n```\n\nIf a type didn't change, the old index is reused.\n\n### Configuration Translation\n\nWhen generators compute Envoy configuration, they consult `PushContext` to:\n\n1. **Resolve service names** to service definitions via `ServiceIndex`\n2. **Apply routing rules** — Find matching `VirtualServices` and `DestinationRules`\n3. **Compute load balancing** — Consult `destinationRuleIndex` for connection pool and outlier detection\n4. **Filter routes** — Check `sidecarIndex` to determine what traffic a proxy should see\n5. **Apply policies** — Consult `AuthzPolicies`, `AuthnPolicies`, `Telemetry`\n6. **Extend config** — Apply `EnvoyFilters` and `WasmPlugins`\n\nExample: Translating a `VirtualService` to Envoy `RouteConfiguration`:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/routes.go` (not shown here but referenced)\n- Reads route rules from the VirtualService CRD\n- Consults `ServiceIndex` to resolve destination service hosts\n- Looks up `DestinationRule` for the destination\n- Generates Envoy `Route` with backend cluster names, weights, retries, etc.\n\n### Push Metrics and Error Tracking\n\n`PushContext` also tracks push status:\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n    // Keyed by error code (e.g., \"success\", \"timeout\"), then by proxy ID\n}\n\ntype ProxyPushStatus struct {\n    ProxyID       string\n    LastUpdateTime time.Time\n    LastError     string\n}\n```\n\nAfter each push to a proxy:\n- Success → recorded in `ProxyStatus[\"success\"]`\n- Error → recorded in `ProxyStatus[errorCode]` with error message\n- Metrics → aggregated and exposed on debug endpoints\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Files:** `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go`, `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller.go`\n\n### Service Discovery Architecture\n\nPilot abstracts service discovery behind a **registry** interface. The system supports multiple registries simultaneously:\n\n```go\ntype ServiceDiscovery interface {\n    Services() []*Service\n    GetService(hostname host.Name) *Service\n    InstancesByPort(hostname host.Name, port int, labels labels.Instance) []*IstioEndpoint\n    // ... etc\n}\n```\n\n### Aggregate Controller Pattern\n\nThe `Controller` in `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/` implements multi-cluster and multi-provider support:\n\n```go\ntype Controller struct {\n    registries []*registryEntry  // List of service registries (K8s, ServiceEntry, etc.)\n    handlers   model.ControllerHandlers  // Callbacks for changes\n}\n```\n\nWhen querying services:\n```go\nfunc (c *Controller) Services() []*Service {\n    var services []*Service\n    for _, reg := range c.registries {\n        services = append(services, reg.Services()...)\n    }\n    return services\n}\n```\n\nThis allows seamless aggregation of:\n- **Kubernetes registries** — One per cluster connected to this Istiod\n- **ServiceEntry resources** — Custom services defined in the mesh\n- **External service discovery** — Pluggable external systems\n\n### Kubernetes Registry\n\nThe main registry implementation for Kubernetes:\n- File: `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller.go`\n\nWatches:\n1. **Services** — Kubernetes `Service` objects\n2. **Endpoints** — `Endpoints` or `EndpointSlices` objects (pod membership)\n3. **Pods** — Pod objects for labels and locality information\n\nWhen a service is created/updated:\n- `SvcUpdate()` is called with the change event\n- Triggers a `PushRequest` with `ConfigsUpdated` including `kind.Service`\n- Next push will regenerate service indices and push CDS/EDS to all proxies\n\nWhen endpoints change (pod scale-up, health check failure):\n- `EDSUpdate()` is called with the updated endpoint list\n- Triggers an incremental `PushRequest` with `Full: false`\n- Only EDS is regenerated; other resource types reuse cached versions\n\n### ServiceEntry Resources\n\nServiceEntry is an Istio CRD that defines custom services:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: ServiceEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: my-service\nspec:\n  hosts:\n  - my-service.example.com\n  location: MESH_EXTERNAL\n  ports:\n  - number: 443\n    name: https\n  endpoints:\n  - address: 1.2.3.4\n    ports:\n      https: 443\n```\n\nServiceEntry acts as a \"service\" in the registry, allowing Istio to mesh traffic to external systems.\n\nA config controller watches ServiceEntry resources and calls `SvcUpdate()` when they change.\n\n### Multi-Cluster Support\n\nMulti-cluster deployments have multiple Istiod instances, each connected to one or more Kubernetes clusters. The aggregate controller handles this:\n\n```go\ntype registryEntry struct {\n    Controller model.ServiceDiscovery\n    clusterID  cluster.ID\n}\n```\n\nEach registry entry has a `clusterID`. When aggregating services:\n\n1. Services are tagged with their source cluster\n2. Endpoints include cluster locality information\n3. The aggregate controller optionally filters by cluster (e.g., for sidecar scope)\n\n**Example:** A gateway in cluster A wants to load-balance across services in clusters A, B, and C:\n- The aggregate controller returns services from all three clusters\n- Each service's endpoints are tagged with their cluster ID\n- Envoy uses cluster-aware load balancing (locality-weighted) to prefer local endpoints\n\n### Push Trigger Points\n\nThe registry triggers pushes at two levels:\n\n**1. Service Changes → Full Config Push**\n```go\ns.XDSUpdater.SvcUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, event)\n// Creates PushRequest with ConfigsUpdated = {kind.Service}\n// → Triggers InitContext to rebuild service indices\n// → Pushes CDS/RDS/EDS to all proxies\n```\n\n**2. Endpoint Changes → Incremental EDS Push**\n```go\ns.XDSUpdater.EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, endpoints)\n// Creates PushRequest with Full: false (incremental)\n// → Skips InitContext; reuses existing PushContext\n// → Pushes only EDS to affected proxies\n```\n\nThis separation is crucial for performance. Endpoint churn (pods scaling, health changes) happens frequently but only affects EDS, not routing rules.\n\n### Error Handling in Registry\n\nIf a registry fails to return services:\n- The error is logged\n- The previous service list is retained (safe-by-default)\n- Subsequent queries will retry\n- Eventually a new push will regenerate the context\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow: From Config Change to Proxy\n\nTo understand how everything works together, trace a typical flow:\n\n### Scenario: VirtualService is created\n\n1. **Controller watches CRD:**\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/config/crd/crd.go` or `pilot/pkg/config/kube/` (config watchers)\n   - Detects new VirtualService in etcd\n   - Calls `ConfigUpdater.ConfigUpdate()`\n\n2. **Push request enters debouncer:**\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:299-319`\n   - `ConfigUpdate()` sends to `pushChannel`\n   - `handleUpdates()` waits for quiet time\n\n3. **Push is triggered:**\n   - File: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go:258-283`\n   - `Push()` calls `initPushContext()` which:\n     - Creates new `PushContext`\n     - Calls `InitContext()` to rebuild indices\n     - `initVirtualServices()` reads all VirtualServices from config store\n   - Calls `AdsPushAll()` to queue push for all proxies\n\n4. **Each proxy receives update:**\n   - `StartPush()` enqueues event for proxy in `pushQueue`\n   - `sendPushes()` calls `pushConnection()` for proxy\n   - `pushConnection()` calls generators:\n     - CDS generator reads services and produces clusters\n     - RDS generator reads VirtualServices and DestinationRules, produces routes\n   - xDS response is sent to proxy via gRPC stream\n\n5. **Proxy processes:**\n   - Envoy receives new routes\n   - Updates its routing table\n   - Traffic is now routed according to the new VirtualService\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### 1. Custom Resource Generators\n\nReplace the default xDS generators to customize Envoy configuration:\n\n```go\ndiscoveryServer.Generators[\"my-custom-generator/cds\"] = myCustomCDSGenerator\n```\n\nCustom generators implement the `XdsResourceGenerator` interface.\n\n### 2. Custom Service Registries\n\nPlug in external service discovery:\n\n```go\naggregateController.AddRegistry(myServiceRegistry, clusterID)\n```\n\nThe aggregate controller will include services from your registry in queries.\n\n### 3. Config Watchers\n\nAdd watchers for custom resources:\n\n```go\nconfigStore.RegisterEventHandler(configUpdateHandler)\n// Handler receives ConfigUpdate events\n```\n\nPush requests will include your resource in `ConfigsUpdated`, triggering regeneration.\n\n### 4. Proxy Filtering\n\nControl which proxies need a push:\n\n```go\ndiscoveryServer.ProxyNeedsPush = myProxyFilter\n```\n\nYour filter can return early if a push is unnecessary for a specific proxy.\n\n### 5. Telemetry and Monitoring\n\nHook into push status:\n\n```go\npush.AddMetric(metric, key, proxyID, message)\n```\n\nMetrics are exposed on debug endpoints and in logs.\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Configuration Validation Errors\n\nWhen a config CRD is invalid (malformed YAML, validation failure):\n- Config controller logs the error\n- The invalid config is not added to the config store\n- Existing proxies retain their previous configuration\n- No push is triggered\n\nThis prevents invalid configs from breaking the mesh.\n\n### Push Generation Errors\n\nIf a generator fails (e.g., out of memory):\n- The error is caught in `pushConnection()`\n- A `DiscoveryResponse` with error status is sent to the proxy\n- The error is recorded in `PushContext.ProxyStatus`\n- The proxy stays connected; next push will retry\n- Error metrics are incremented\n\n### Registry Errors\n\nIf a service registry becomes unavailable:\n- Queries return cached services\n- Subsequent changes trigger retries\n- Eventually the registry recovers and new changes are processed\n\n### Proxy Connection Errors\n\nIf a proxy becomes unresponsive:\n- The stream is closed\n- The connection is removed from `adsClients`\n- The `WorkloadEntryController` is notified (cleanup auto-registered proxies)\n- Other proxies continue receiving pushes unaffected\n\n---\n\n## Performance and Scalability Considerations\n\n### Debouncing\n\nPrevents sending 100 pushes when 100 configs change in rapid succession. Instead, one debounced push is sent after quiet time.\n\nTunable via:\n- `DebounceAfter` — Quiet time threshold (default: 100ms)\n- `debounceMax` — Maximum wait time (default: 10s)\n- `enableEDSDebounce` — Whether to debounce EDS separately\n\n### Concurrent Push Limiting\n\nSemaphore prevents overwhelming CPU/memory by sending to all 10,000 proxies simultaneously.\n\nTunable via:\n- `PushThrottle` — Max concurrent pushes (default: 100)\n\n### Caching\n\nGenerated Envoy configuration is cached in `PushContext.Cache`. If nothing changed, the cache hit avoids recomputation.\n\n### Incremental Updates\n\nEDS changes don't regenerate routing configuration. Endpoint churn is common; full pushes are expensive.\n\n### Resource Indexes\n\n`PushContext` builds indices (maps) of services, VirtualServices, etc. for O(1) lookup instead of O(n) scanning.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\nCore implementation:\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` — DiscoveryServer lifecycle and push coordination\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` — ADS stream handling and per-proxy pushes\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/delta.go` — Delta XDS alternative protocol\n- `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` — PushContext initialization and indices\n- `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` — Environment and global push context management\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/aggregate/controller.go` — Multi-registry aggregation\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/kube/controller.go` — Kubernetes service discovery\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/configgen.go` — ConfigGenerator interface definition\n- `pilot/pkg/bootstrap/server.go` — Pilot server initialization and controller setup\n\nConfig and CRD handling:\n- `pilot/pkg/config/crd/crd.go` — CRD config store\n- `pilot/pkg/config/kube/` — Kubernetes resource controllers\n\nGenerators (xDS resource translation):\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/` — VirtualService, DestinationRule translation\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` — Cluster Discovery Service (CDS) generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` — Route Discovery Service (RDS) generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` — Listener Discovery Service (LDS) generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` — Endpoint Discovery Service (EDS) generator\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nPilot's discovery service is a coordinated system where:\n\n- **DiscoveryServer** manages the overall push flow, debouncing, and concurrency\n- **ADS** handles individual proxy connections and request/response streams\n- **PushContext** provides a consistent, immutable configuration snapshot\n- **ServiceRegistry** feeds real-time services and endpoints into the context\n\nConfiguration changes trigger a push that flows through debouncing, context regeneration, resource generation, and broadcasting to all proxies. The architecture supports multi-cluster deployments, incremental updates, error recovery, and extensive customization through generators and filters.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
